 * Terminal — PowerShell-style terminal interface
 * All colors via CSS variables (var(--sd-*))
 * Ported from simdecisions-2 to browser/src/primitives/terminal/
 */

/**
 * Terminal Error Styling — error messages, warnings, and suggestions
 * Used by errorClassifier and errorMessages modules
 */

/* Error messages */

.terminal-error {
  color: var(--sd-red);
  font-weight: 500;
  margin: 8px 0;
  white-space: pre-wrap;
  word-break: break-word;
}

/* Error suggestion text */

.terminal-error-suggestion {
  color: var(--sd-text-secondary);
  margin-top: 4px;
  font-style: italic;
  font-size: 13px;
}

/* Warning messages */

.terminal-warning {
  color: var(--sd-yellow);
  font-weight: 500;
  margin: 8px 0;
  white-space: pre-wrap;
  word-break: break-word;
}

/* Main terminal container */

.terminal-pane {
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: column;
  flex: 1;
  min-height: 0;
  background: var(--sd-bg);
  color: var(--sd-text-primary);
  font-family: 'JetBrains Mono', 'Cascadia Code', 'Consolas', monospace;
  overflow: hidden;
}

/* Compact mode — prompt + status bar only, no flex expansion */

.terminal-pane--compact {
  flex: 0 0 auto;
  justify-content: flex-end;
}

/* Minimal mode — 2-line input + system message only */

.terminal-pane--minimal {
  flex: 0 0 auto;
  justify-content: flex-end;
  min-height: auto;
}

.terminal-status-bar {

}
